 <h2><br></h2>
 <h2>3.《香蜜沉沉烬如霜》</h2>
 <p data-pid="unymZWDF">旭风母亲天后将润玉母亲杀死后,旭凤主动找润玉喝酒说：“我母亲将你母亲杀害,我在这里向你赔罪了。”所以杀母之仇是一句赔罪就可以解决的？而且他的重点是希望润玉解除与锦觅的婚约,赔礼道歉只是顺便，在人家丧母的时候要人家原谅杀人凶手还要抢人家未婚妻，吼……</p>

 <h2>4.①《一起来看流星雨》</h2>
 <h2>②台版《流星花园》</h2>
 <h2>③新版《流星花园》</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0ce1f40d1c7eb5675fae2edd56a231cf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="390" data-rawheight="358" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-0ce1f40d1c7eb5675fae2edd56a231cf" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d8dcdb3ddff2348ebd7188eaaec7a2fc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="390">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="HcBzh1MH"><b><i>有钱长得帅是我的错吗？</i></b></p>
 <p data-pid="zlzdyQLD">不是，是我们错了，对不起。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">

 </figure>
 <h2><br></h2>
 <h2>5.《又见一帘幽梦》</h2>
 <p data-pid="6PEDvI8c"><b>看看这些男人说的是人话吗？</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-96e792c639f40a610931a4f564dea066_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="520" data-rawheight="300" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-96e792c639f40a610931a4f564dea066" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5a793e5deb83ee91a59e506d71a43b99_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="520" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-96e792c639f40a610931a4f564dea066_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3ad24ff98834deb2cd1f748c7b702a29_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="480" data-rawheight="593" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-3ad24ff98834deb2cd1f748c7b702a29" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-41b53f493d9b34c138ca8686e78a1f17_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="480" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-3ad24ff98834deb2cd1f748c7b702a29_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="KOArT9bT">紫荆学习不行，家里给特殊关照找的工作她也迟到早退，上司说她两句，结果人家辞职了。天呐真是有骨气的女孩子呢！</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-213dd746d698a75095e43578291a5c79_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="531" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-213dd746d698a75095e43578291a5c79" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a424cda29115d5caadcb172699513d14_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-213dd746d698a75095e43578291a5c79_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="TvwfH8Ia">紫菱好可怜呢，十六岁就暗恋姐夫了，姐夫都不看她只关注姐姐好过分！还好，楚濂发现自己的真爱其实是紫菱。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6be74a9581bbdc36f330a398aa63fe7c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="464" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-6be74a9581bbdc36f330a398aa63fe7c" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-71d3d1f781b2901d225b3ec31b91826a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6be74a9581bbdc36f330a398aa63fe7c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="4rlt_fHP">对于移情别恋，楚濂是这么说的：如果两个人没有真正爱过，那又怎么称得上是移情别恋呢？那你当初追人绿萍干嘛！</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-ef69f6757a337fdaa866a7a4ba7b21e2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="418" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-ef69f6757a337fdaa866a7a4ba7b21e2" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b054b66ce44b8ac12b7b8f11864a66d4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef69f6757a337fdaa866a7a4ba7b21e2_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="rbiu-wR4">之后楚濂开车载着绿萍出了车祸，绿萍腿断了，不能跳舞了。他也没道歉。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-d3e181168bc71b71c8b0c3834bf7e14b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="358" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-d3e181168bc71b71c8b0c3834bf7e14b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5686090306832f6351b4a4dcd1408c7d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d3e181168bc71b71c8b0c3834bf7e14b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="abyYSlwN">紫菱的爸爸对得知真相的绿萍说，哪怕牺牲紫菱，也会让楚濂娶你。（牺牲？）</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-4623c191b295753209cdb7fe35585255_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="359" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-4623c191b295753209cdb7fe35585255" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-08294410a2ac7194aedeb1e7ae90a36c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-4623c191b295753209cdb7fe35585255_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>6.《家有儿女》</h2>
 <p data-pid="QP9sCqjk">第一部第38集，我是忍不了了。</p>
 <p data-pid="ugbzlTnS">他救了被打的二胖，刘梅没夸他，还冷落他夸小雪，第二次他没救，二胖家长和刘梅告状（人家救你不是理所当然吧？）刘梅立马就生气了要打骂刘星。小雪指出了刘梅的错误，刘梅道歉了又说刘星没救二胖不对，要全家去二胖家道歉？？？</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8e9ec66fc0421d4d09e187d65f46e1cf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="2280" data-rawheight="1080" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-8e9ec66fc0421d4d09e187d65f46e1cf" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e97a09470d09016fa2b099a2bf8669b5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2280" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-8e9ec66fc0421d4d09e187d65f46e1cf_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <h2>还有几张图哈哈哈</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aGFDrwnY">听不懂听不懂……</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-30f91e3ff4f75509dc9c6f2ef8e6712f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="2340" data-rawheight="1080" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-30f91e3ff4f75509dc9c6f2ef8e6712f" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-2c13384385a343bd8ff633f0c7256ffe_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2340" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-30f91e3ff4f75509dc9c6f2ef8e6712f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d9f122c16d81c37a13996d7df64fe46d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="2340" data-rawheight="1080" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-d9f122c16d81c37a13996d7df64fe46d" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-06fc38f3c651a2d93552f848529ea4b5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2340" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d9f122c16d81c37a13996d7df64fe46d_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DiRjuHUv"><b>《龙门镖局》</b>这个听说是故意搞笑的很好看，那我有时间也去看看，毕竟陈晓帅。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-df984c146ee50234901d26e80f216019_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="412" data-rawheight="228" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-df984c146ee50234901d26e80f216019" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-198ceb76939bc0a43ab5af33aff2e29e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="412">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eNyGfiRc"><b>《欢乐颂》</b></p>
 <p data-pid="i-HpV9js">看见安迪开豪车，就恶意揣测。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-cc7687706da621462168a7623312c2d0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="700" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-cc7687706da621462168a7623312c2d0" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9dab5b27dc99652972a593cf51bb6bdc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-cc7687706da621462168a7623312c2d0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="-hGGqsU4">为了让安迪帮忙，又买着礼物去道歉。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8280e395488a03962101368b9fd41598_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="490" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-8280e395488a03962101368b9fd41598" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-54cb5664c857b65f95a7999aab4b22fb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-8280e395488a03962101368b9fd41598_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="lyxYvtI2">往小蚯蚓男友口袋里塞纸条，还说是为了考验她男友，明明是为了证明自己的魅力，却好像是在大发善心。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6535357736fa8ef858e50bca75e8602c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="394" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-6535357736fa8ef858e50bca75e8602c" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f0bc398a5f6f159ec568591b0329b0f0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-6535357736fa8ef858e50bca75e8602c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="GFES93C_">看上赵医生之后说，只要赵医生未婚，一切都不是问题。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6e2ef3a6eff9e14e1a5e4dad99917a11_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="410" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-6e2ef3a6eff9e14e1a5e4dad99917a11" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-62b70ee4219a43f6bf05bb936721a697_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-6e2ef3a6eff9e14e1a5e4dad99917a11_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="O8im5oaX">说好的平生最恨小三小四呢？</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c2ac1d2b3d174ac83e617e50828e84d4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="363" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-c2ac1d2b3d174ac83e617e50828e84d4" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1b12ba789ab851740d8bb591cdbb3d18_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-c2ac1d2b3d174ac83e617e50828e84d4_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m8evNxjL">《小丈夫》</p>
 <p data-pid="2i--n9Md">男主不管捅了什么篓子都要跟家里要钱，张口闭口钱都是他的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-425c4df7a0d90d96e1801f3835dda3f9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="807" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-425c4df7a0d90d96e1801f3835dda3f9" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6758723eca7ef0f812ec887ee7814727_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-425c4df7a0d90d96e1801f3835dda3f9_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="HL_uteVY">还盼着他姐出轨，自己带姐夫去捉奸，好抓到他姐的把柄...这是正常人么各位。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-58631c164bed013ace8f3392a7c3b318_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="399" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-58631c164bed013ace8f3392a7c3b318" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e432de7121fccd39ae7f85d7bfdf2097_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-58631c164bed013ace8f3392a7c3b318_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T8SHEpdw">《奋斗》</p>
 <p data-pid="x3Y5U1U9">男主角陆涛劈腿了女友的闺蜜。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-cc8f87701b61cda2dfb21c5aab2cfd8b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="392" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-cc8f87701b61cda2dfb21c5aab2cfd8b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-42ab7f7a7579d44d9f7f85e3edc75811_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-cc8f87701b61cda2dfb21c5aab2cfd8b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="I_gddiV-">前脚跟米莱分开，后脚就跟夏琳调情。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e88d714d1d5c058f418cbb78e719e97a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="395" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-e88d714d1d5c058f418cbb78e719e97a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-14d9b7f7b2782287331ab9cfe1a5e200_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-e88d714d1d5c058f418cbb78e719e97a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="6sZHUhVQ">紧接着俩人出来去了陆涛家，他告白了。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-38f405351f61af4263eab7ee9d0f3c2f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="1189" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-38f405351f61af4263eab7ee9d0f3c2f" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-87493e630e01663bc3a91e095ce96d08_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-38f405351f61af4263eab7ee9d0f3c2f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <h2>5.《神探狄仁杰》</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ab616895c61015f5576181cce2fd6e84_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="354" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-ab616895c61015f5576181cce2fd6e84" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c8c8a6f5e3242885a28428fdf1896a4e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ab616895c61015f5576181cce2fd6e84_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-6b8d7f004a24a44e3dd93f50608088f1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="551" data-rawheight="360" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-6b8d7f004a24a44e3dd93f50608088f1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c6f665e06e082601185ac57d8a1217c1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="551" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-6b8d7f004a24a44e3dd93f50608088f1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="dsJKY7RK"><b><i>如果是自杀那她的动机肯定是不想活了。</i></b></p>
 <p data-pid="5ORJNe65">我们元芳的搞笑天赋也是很强的嘛！</p>
 <h2>7.《水浒传》</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a227ab27a6754fb83e0d7a99a421e5be_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="466" data-rawheight="551" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-a227ab27a6754fb83e0d7a99a421e5be" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-dc33b9faa3ca2ef0cd8a042fac5623ab_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="466" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a227ab27a6754fb83e0d7a99a421e5be_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="BSZs3mDB"><b><i>智深，以后就到我的房间去睡吧。</i></b></p>
 <p data-pid="-z9F_GQ6">宋朝时期，中国就已经很开放了。</p>
